***означать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:означать.html>означа́ть</a> (1330)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">озна́чить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oznáčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:означать.html>означа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">označátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">озна́чить</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to mean, to signify</li>
<li>to stand for, to represent, to betoken, to denote</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The perfective form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">озна́чить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oznáčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is now dated.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:значить.html>зна́чить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">znáčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обозначать.html>обознача́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">oboznačátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выражать.html>выража́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vyražátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">помеча́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pomečátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обозначать.html>обознача́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">oboznačátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знак.html>знак</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">znak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обозначение.html>обозначе́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">oboznačénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оказавшийся.html>оказа́вшийся</a> (181)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оказавшийся.html>оказа́вшийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okazávšijsja</span>)

***оказать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оказать.html>оказа́ть</a> (3511)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казать.html>каза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оказать.html>оказа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okazátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оказывать.html>ока́зывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to show, to render, to do, to provide (help, service, support, etc.)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оказать.html>оказа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okazátʹ</b> uslúgu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to do / render somebody a service</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to exert (influence)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оказать.html>оказа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:влияние.html>влия́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okazátʹ</b> vlijánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to influence, to exert influence</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to put, to exert (pressure)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оказать.html>оказа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:давление.html>давле́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okazátʹ</b> davlénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put pressure</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to accord (respect)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оказать.html>оказа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:почтение.html>почте́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okazátʹ</b> počténije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to treat with respect</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to offer (resistance)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оказать.html>оказа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сопротивление.html>сопротивле́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okazátʹ</b> soprotivlénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to offer resistance</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to give (somebody a reception)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оказать.html>оказа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:холодный.html>холо́дный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прием.html>приём</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okazátʹ</b> xolódnyj prijóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cold-shoulder</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оказать.html>оказа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">okazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>
<ol><li>to turn out, to be found, to prove (to be)</li>

<li><i>in expressions</i>

***оказывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оказывать.html>ока́зывать</a> (3717)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оказать.html>оказа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">okazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оказывать.html>ока́зывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okázyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оказать.html>оказа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to show, to render, to do, to provide <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">help, service, support, etc.</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оказывать.html>ока́зывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okázyvatʹ</b> uslúgu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to do / render somebody a service</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оказывать.html>ока́зывайте</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:начинающий.html>начина́ющему</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:водитель.html>води́телю</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okázyvajte</b> pómoščʹ načinájuščemu vodítelju.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Provide help to the inexperienced driver.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to exert <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">influence</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оказывать.html>ока́зывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:влияние.html>влия́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okázyvatʹ</b> vlijánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to influence, to exert influence</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to put, to exert (pressure)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оказывать.html>ока́зывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:давление.html>давле́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okázyvatʹ</b> davlénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put pressure</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to accord (respect)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оказывать.html>ока́зывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:почтение.html>почте́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okázyvatʹ</b> počténije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to treat with respect</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to offer (resistance)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оказывать.html>ока́зывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сопротивление.html>сопротивле́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okázyvatʹ</b> soprotivlénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to offer resistance</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to give (somebody a reception)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оказывать.html>ока́зывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:холодный.html>холо́дный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прием.html>приём</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okázyvatʹ</b> xolódnyj prijóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cold-shoulder</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оказывать.html>ока́зывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">okázyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оказываться.html>ока́зываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okázyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оказаться.html>оказа́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn out, to be found, to prove (to be)</li>
<li>to find oneself</li>
<li>to be found</li>
<li><i>in expressions</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оказываться.html>ока́зываться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́сом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okázyvatʹsja</b> pod voprósom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be called into question</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оказывать.html>ока́зывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">okázyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***окаймлённый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:окаймлённый.html>окаймлённый</a> (23768)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окаймлённый.html>окаймлённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okajmljónnyj</span>)
</p>

***окаменелый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:окаменелый.html>окамене́лый</a> (31719)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окаменеть.html>окамене́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">okamenétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окаменелый.html>окамене́лый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okamenélyj</span>) (<i>rare comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)окамене́лее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)окамене́лей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>petrified, turned to stone</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> petrified <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with fear, shock, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>hardened, embittered, unfeeling</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<ul><li>The comparative is rare and found mostly in poetry.</li></ul>
